| **Learning / Self‑Heal** | • Last learned: “User‑visible surfaces drifted from swarm logic”. <br>• Last self‑fix applied: audit failure in cycle 1 (the system recognized the audit mismatch and logged it). |

### Key Take‑aways
1. **Account data is currently stale** – the live API is rate‑limited, so the swarm is operating on a cached snapshot. This limits confidence in the reported equity/available margin.
2. **Both open shorts lack TP/SL** and are blocked from further short additions. Immediate action: place TP/SL for `BAS‑USDT` and `VELVET‑USDT` using `blofin_place_tpsl` / `blofin_ensure_position_tpsl`.
3. **Available margin (≈ 0.42 USDT) is very low** relative to equity; new positions are unlikely to be funded until margin frees up or equity grows.
4. **Rate‑limit handling**: the system should back‑off, use cached data, and retry the balance endpoint after a cooldown (≈ 120 s) to avoid further 429s.
5. **No new trade candidates** are currently viable because the only short candidates are blocked; the swarm should scan the broader universe for a fresh, unblocked symbol or skip the trade this cycle per the enforced rules.

| **Account balances** | **Equity = $0.00**, **Available = $0.00** – both zero because the live API returned an empty response. |
| **Last error** | None recorded in state, but a **rate‑limit (HTTP 429)** error occurred when trying to fetch balance (`/api/v1/account/balance`). |
| **Log highlights** | • Loop interval 90 s – LLM cycle started.<br>• Task board seeded, cycle init persisted.<br>• Pre‑flight and ops‑monitor started in background.<br>• Pentest‑squad armed (watchdog).<br>• **WARN:** “Account refresh: live API empty – using disk snapshot”. |
| **Universe** | 511 symbols loaded from `chromium_ws`; cache age 68 s. |
| **Portfolio** | • **1 open position** – `VELVET‑USDT` short, size = ‑1.<br>• Avg. price = 1.5412, mark price = 1.49744, unrealized PnL ≈ +0.438 USDT.<br>• Position is **blocked for new sells** (cannot add to short).<br>• **Missing TP/SL** for this position. |
| **Rules enforced** | 1. No new buys on blocked‑buy list (empty).<br>2. No new sells on blocked‑sell list (`VELVET‑USDT`).<br>3. If the only candidate is blocked → skip trade.<br>4. | **Equity‑error detail** | HTTP 429 (Cloudflare 1015) – rate‑limited when requesting account balance. |
| **Learning / self‑heal** | • Swarm learned that “User‑visible surfaces drifted from swarm logic”.<br>• Last self‑fix: “Task audit failed cycle 1”. |

### Key Insights & Immediate Actions
1. **Zero equity/available** is *not* a true account state – it is a fallback because the live balance API was rate‑limited. The system is currently using a disk snapshot, which may be stale.  
2. **Rate‑limit (429)** must be mitigated:
   - Back‑off API calls, use cached balance for the remainder of the cycle.  
   - Schedule a cooldown (≈ 2 min) before the next balance request.  
3. **Open short on VELVET‑USDT** lacks TP/SL → must place them immediately (`blofin_place_tpsl` or `blofin_ensure_position_tpsl`).  
4. Because VELVET‑USDT is on the *blocked‑sell* list, no additional short orders can be added this cycle; the swarm should either:
   - Scan the universe for another tradable symbol, **or**  
   - Skip new trades for this cycle if no eligible candidate exists.  
5. **Pentest‑squad** is active; any further API‑rate‑limit spikes will be caught by the watchdog. Ensure the watchdog logs the cooldown and that the cache is refreshed after the limit lifts.  

### Recommended Immediate Fixes (to be auto‑executed)
- **Apply TP/SL** to `VELVET‑USDT` now.  
- **Enter API‑cooldown mode** for balance calls (e.g., 120 s back‑off) and rely on the cached snapshot until the limit clears.  
- **Refresh universe cache** after cooldown to guarantee fresh symbol data.  
- **Audit task board** to confirm no phantom trades were marked done without order IDs (the self‑heal log indicates a prior audit failure).  

These steps will bring the stack back to a **healthy** state, resolve the missing TP/SL, and prevent further 429‑induced stalls.
